var g0041s6HasSearchQuery;
function g0041s6SetSearchQuery(hasSearchQuery, search_queryValue) {
var search_query = document.searchbox.search_query;
if (hasSearchQuery) {
g0041s6HasSearchQuery = true;
search_query.value = search_queryValue;
search_query.style.color = "#333333";
}
else {
g0041s6HasSearchQuery = false;
search_query.value = "Search";
search_query.style.color = "#999999";
}
}
g0041s6SetSearchQuery(WALMART.page.search_query, WALMART.page.search_query);
WALMART.page.g0041s6 = {
validate: function () {
if (!g0041s6HasSearchQuery) {
document.searchbox.search_query.value = "";
}
return true;
}
, focus: function () {
if (!g0041s6HasSearchQuery) {
g0041s6SetSearchQuery(true, "");
}
}
, blur: function () {
if (document.searchbox.search_query.value.length == 0) {
g0041s6SetSearchQuery(false);
}
}
, submit: function () {
return WALMART.page.g0041s6.validate() && document.searchbox.submit();
}
, set: function (value) {
g0041s6SetSearchQuery(value, value);
}
}

<div class="BVRRSContentDiv"><h1 class="BVRRSProductHeaderBar"><span class="BVRRSStandaloneHeaderBarLabel">Customer Reviews for Graco Graco - MyRide 65 Convertible Car Seat, Cuddle</span></h1><div id="BVRRSExternalSubjectID" class="BVRRSExternalSubject"><div id="BVExternalSubjectImageID" class="BVRRSExternalSubjectImage"><a href="http://www.walmart.com/catalog/product.do?product_id=15642055" title="Graco - MyRide 65 Convertible Car Seat, Cuddle" onclick="javascript:gaPageTracker._trackPageview('/outgoing/product/15642055')"><img alt="Graco - MyRide 65 Convertible Car Seat, Cuddle" src="http://i.walmartimages.com/i/p/00/04/74/06/11/0004740611060_100X100.jpg"
itemprop="image" onerror="if(!this.bvNoImage){this.bvNoImage=true;this.src='http://walmart.ugc.bazaarvoice.com/static/1336/noimage100.gif';}return true;" />
</a></div><div id="BVRRSExternalSubjectDataID" class="BVRRSExternalSubjectData">
<h3 id="BVRRSExternalSubjectTitleID" class="BVRRSExternalSubjectTitle">
<a href="http://www.walmart.com/catalog/product.do?product_id=15642055" title="Graco Graco - MyRide 65 Convertible Car Seat, Cuddle" onclick="javascript:gaPageTracker._trackPageview('/outgoing/product/15642055')"><span id="BVRRSExternalSubjectTitleBrandID" class="BVRRSExternalSubjectTitleBrand">Graco</span> <span id="BVRRSExternalSubjectTitleProductNameID" itemprop="name" class="BVRRSExternalSubjectTitleProductName">Graco - MyRide 65 Convertible Car Seat, Cuddle</span></a> </h3>
<div id="BVRRSExternalSubjectDescriptionID" itemprop="description" class="BVRRSExternalSubjectDescription">Keep your growing child safe with the Graco MyRide 65 Convertible Car Seat. The American Academy of Pediatrics recommends that your child ride rear-facing as long as possible. The MyRide 65 stays rear-facing longer than most other infant car safety seats. Carry this car seat even when traveling by air as it is approved to be used in airplanes. The Graco infant car seat is meticulously side-impact and crash tested so that it not only meets but exceeds the safety standards set by US government. Energy absorbing foam and EPS results in efficient collision management whereby offering extra safety. During journeys children are kept comfortable and snug with the help of the detachable toddler headrest and insert. The front adjustable and 5-point harness aids in getting children inside and outside the car seat easily. This convertible baby car seat is outfitted with a latch having a user friendly level indicator that assists you to install it without any hassles.</div>

<div class="BVRRReviewTextContainer"><div class="BVRRReviewTextParagraph BVRRReviewTextFirstParagraph BVRRReviewTextLastParagraph"><span itemprop="description" class="BVRRReviewText">I recently purchased the Graco My Ride 65 Cuddle. She and I both love this seat. I love it because she looks super comfy and extra safe. I already knew before I bought it that it was a bigger seat. That was OK with me. I put it right in my vehicle and we were good to go! The print is super cute and fabric is very soft! I have a Honda Pilot and I am able to put 3 car seats (including this one) all in the middle row! My other 2 have a Cosco seat and a Graco Nautilus. GREAT SEAT!!!! I also love that it rear faces to 40 lbs and front faces to 65!!!! Can't go wrong with this seat!!</span></div></div>

<div class="RRBeforeTitleContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRReviewDateContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewDatePrefix"></span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRReviewDate">09/11/2012<meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2012-09-11"/></span><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewDateSuffix"></span></div>
<div class="RRBeforeUserContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRUserNicknameContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserNicknamePrefix">By </span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRUserNickname"><span itemprop="author" class="BVRRNickname">HeaC </span></span> <span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserNicknameSuffix">,</span>
<div class="BVRRUserLocationContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserLocationPrefix"></span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRUserLocation">SouthEast US</span><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserLocationSuffix"></span></div></div>
<div class="BVRROverallRatingContainer" >
<div class="BVRRRatingContainerStar"><div class="BVRRRatingEntry BVRROdd"><div id="BVRRRatingOverall_Review_Display" class="BVRRRating BVRRRatingNormal BVRRRatingOverall"><div class="BVRRLabel BVRRRatingNormalLabel"></div><div class="BVRRRatingNormalImage">
<div class="BVImgOrSprite" style="width:75px;height:15px;overflow:hidden"><img src="http://walmart.ugc.bazaarvoice.com/1336/5_0/9/rating.png" alt="4 out of 5" title="4 out of 5" width="135" height="15" style="margin-left:-15px" />
</div></div>
<div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" class="BVRRRatingNormalOutOf"> <span itemprop="ratingValue" class="BVRRNumber BVRRRatingNumber">4</span>
<span class="BVRRSeparatorText">out of</span>
<span itemprop="bestRating" class="BVRRNumber BVRRRatingRangeNumber">5</span>
</div></div></div></div> </div>
<div class="RRReviewDisplayStyle2BeforeContentContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRReviewDisplayStyle2ContentContainer">
<div class="BVRRReviewTextContainer"><div class="BVRRReviewTextParagraph BVRRReviewTextFirstParagraph BVRRReviewTextLastParagraph"><span itemprop="description" class="BVRRReviewText">After reading reviews from other buyers, consumer review blogs, etc., I selected the Graco MyRide 65 for my daughter. The seat is attractive, has a good safety review, and met my price range. The seat installation was comparable to my other experiences installing car seats. The car seat is a good bit larger than the traditional backwards-facing car seat in order to accommodate a two-year-old's size. The car seat's larger size leads me to believe that this car seat could not be comfortably installed in a small car or some smaller SUVs. In my minivan, however, this is not a problem. I will note, though, that the size does prohibit anyone from entering on the side of the car seat to the back row. The seat portion of the car seat leans back a lot and is pretty deep, no doubt to ensure the safety of a taller child in the event of a crash. The angle, however, does make getting the child in and out of the car seat a bit tricky until you get the hang of it. I would recommend this seat to people who have a larger SUV or minivan, only want to buy one car seat for their child, and have found other models to be out of their price range.</span></div></div>

Not a huge issue though.<br />Money well spent</span></div></div>

<div class="RRBeforeTitleContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRReviewTitleContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewTitlePrefix"></span> <h2>
<span itemprop="name" class="BVRRValue BVRRReviewTitle">EXACTLY what I wanted</span> </h2>
<span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewTitleSuffix">,</span></div>
<div class="BVRRReviewDateContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewDatePrefix"></span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRReviewDate">08/25/2012<meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2012-08-25"/></span><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewDateSuffix"></span></div>
<div class="RRBeforeUserContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRUserNicknameContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserNicknamePrefix">By </span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRUserNickname"><span itemprop="author" class="BVRRNickname">AmbRRR </span></span> <span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserNicknameSuffix">,</span>
<div class="BVRRUserLocationContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserLocationPrefix"></span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRUserLocation">Olmsted Falls, Ohio</span><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserLocationSuffix"></span></div></div>
<div class="BVRROverallRatingContainer" >
<div class="BVRRRatingContainerStar"><div class="BVRRRatingEntry BVRROdd"><div id="BVRRRatingOverall_Review_Display" class="BVRRRating BVRRRatingNormal BVRRRatingOverall"><div class="BVRRLabel BVRRRatingNormalLabel"></div><div class="BVRRRatingNormalImage">
<div class="BVImgOrSprite" style="width:75px;height:15px;overflow:hidden"><img src="http://walmart.ugc.bazaarvoice.com/1336/5_0/9/rating.png" alt="5 out of 5" title="5 out of 5" width="135" height="15" />
</div></div>
<div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" class="BVRRRatingNormalOutOf"> <span itemprop="ratingValue" class="BVRRNumber BVRRRatingNumber">5</span>
<span class="BVRRSeparatorText">out of</span>
<span itemprop="bestRating" class="BVRRNumber BVRRRatingRangeNumber">5</span>
</div></div></div></div> </div>
<div class="RRReviewDisplayStyle2BeforeContentContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRReviewDisplayStyle2ContentContainer">
<div class="BVRRReviewTextContainer"><div class="BVRRReviewTextParagraph BVRRReviewTextFirstParagraph BVRRReviewTextLastParagraph"><span itemprop="description" class="BVRRReviewText">My fiance and I bought our daughter a Safety 1st Complete Air 65 as her first convertible car seat, but we decided not to use it until we were ready to put our daughter FWD facing and when that time finally came, I only used it ONCE b/c my poor daughter looked SO UNCOMFORTABLE! Her head kind of slouched forward and when she started to fall asleep, her head REALLY hung forward. :-(<br />So I told me fiance that I wanted my own car seat for my car and he could just put that one in his vehicle (my daughter is NEVER w/o me anyway, so we'll always use mine, LoL)! Finally, after LOT'S &amp; LOT'S of research, I decided on the Graco My Ride 65 and it's EXACTLY what I wanted!! My issue's w/the Complete Air were how uncomfortable she appeared and how her head slouched and hung forward and the My Ride is PERFECT for avoiding those issues!! My daughter kind of sits back like she's just relaxing in her own little recliner!! I'm SO HAPPY w/this purchase!! Now, it is a pretty bulky seat (I can only imagine how much room/space it needs when rear facing), but I actually drive a Silverado SS in the summer and the backseat isn't big at all, it's pretty much a bench seat but a lot more cushiony and comfortable than your typical truck back seat, and the My Ride STILL fits back there, in the middle!! If I put her on one of the sides, behind a seat, I can honestly say that Idk how it would affect our sitting situation in the front seat. And when it came to putting the car seat (My Ride) in our vehicle, it was EXTREMELY EASY w/that LATCH system, my fiance just hooked the three spots, pulled them nice and tight, and we were ready to go!! And then when I put my daughter in the seat, it's just as easy to buckle her up as it was w/her infant seat!! Lastly, the My Ride has an AMAZING price as well; $129.00!! You can't beat that! That was literally $70 cheaper than the Complete Air when we bought it! All around, this was a GREAT purchase and I'm BEYOND satisfied! Idk how easy or hard it will be to clean though, especially b/c we got the cuddle and it's almost like a suede material (I can't think of the name of that really soft material that it appears to be), but w/all the other benefits, that's an issue I'm MORE THAN HAPPY to deal with (description says that the cover comes off easily and is machine washable)!! :-)</span></div></div>
<div class="RRRBeforeSecondaryRatingsContainerSpacer"></div>

<div class="BVRRReviewTitleContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewTitlePrefix"></span> <h2>
<span itemprop="name" class="BVRRValue BVRRReviewTitle">Nice comfy seat, though very large!</span> </h2>
<span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewTitleSuffix">,</span></div>
<div class="BVRRReviewDateContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewDatePrefix"></span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRReviewDate">08/23/2012<meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2012-08-23"/></span><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewDateSuffix"></span></div>
<div class="RRBeforeUserContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRUserNicknameContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserNicknamePrefix">By </span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRUserNickname"><span itemprop="author" class="BVRRNickname">OnePleasedMom </span></span> <span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserNicknameSuffix">,</span>
<div class="BVRRUserLocationContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserLocationPrefix"></span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRUserLocation">mt vernon, il</span><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserLocationSuffix"></span></div></div>
<div class="BVRROverallRatingContainer" >
<div class="BVRRRatingContainerStar"><div class="BVRRRatingEntry BVRROdd"><div id="BVRRRatingOverall_Review_Display" class="BVRRRating BVRRRatingNormal BVRRRatingOverall"><div class="BVRRLabel BVRRRatingNormalLabel"></div><div class="BVRRRatingNormalImage">
<div class="BVImgOrSprite" style="width:75px;height:15px;overflow:hidden"><img src="http://walmart.ugc.bazaarvoice.com/1336/5_0/9/rating.png" alt="4 out of 5" title="4 out of 5" width="135" height="15" style="margin-left:-15px" />
</div></div>
<div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" class="BVRRRatingNormalOutOf"> <span itemprop="ratingValue" class="BVRRNumber BVRRRatingNumber">4</span>
<span class="BVRRSeparatorText">out of</span>
<span itemprop="bestRating" class="BVRRNumber BVRRRatingRangeNumber">5</span>
</div></div></div></div> </div>
<div class="RRReviewDisplayStyle2BeforeContentContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRReviewDisplayStyle2ContentContainer">
<div class="BVRRReviewTextContainer"><div class="BVRRReviewTextParagraph BVRRReviewTextFirstParagraph BVRRReviewTextLastParagraph"><span itemprop="description" class="BVRRReviewText">This seat is super plush and soft for baby. The insert cushions are only useable with the first and second level of shoulder strap, which were too low for my one year old. Cup holders are nice to have and buckles are easy to use. This seat is very large, so it may be a very tight squeeze in a smaller vehicle. We are using the seat in the forward facing position. I am not sure we would have been able to use it in the rear facing position in my explorer because it is so large. Overall I am happy with the seat and just hope it washes well in the future!</span></div></div>

<div class="RRBeforeTitleContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRReviewTitleContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewTitlePrefix"></span> <h2>
<span itemprop="name" class="BVRRValue BVRRReviewTitle">Comfy and sturdy seat for the price</span> </h2>
<span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewTitleSuffix">,</span></div>
<div class="BVRRReviewDateContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewDatePrefix"></span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRReviewDate">07/30/2012<meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2012-07-30"/></span><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewDateSuffix"></span></div>
<div class="RRBeforeUserContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRUserNicknameContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserNicknamePrefix">By </span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRUserNickname"><span itemprop="author" class="BVRRNickname">lovetravelgirl </span></span> <span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserNicknameSuffix">,</span>
<div class="BVRRUserLocationContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserLocationPrefix"></span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRUserLocation">Minneapolis, MN</span><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserLocationSuffix"></span></div></div>
<div class="BVRROverallRatingContainer" >
<div class="BVRRRatingContainerStar"><div class="BVRRRatingEntry BVRROdd"><div id="BVRRRatingOverall_Review_Display" class="BVRRRating BVRRRatingNormal BVRRRatingOverall"><div class="BVRRLabel BVRRRatingNormalLabel"></div><div class="BVRRRatingNormalImage">
<div class="BVImgOrSprite" style="width:75px;height:15px;overflow:hidden"><img src="http://walmart.ugc.bazaarvoice.com/1336/5_0/9/rating.png" alt="4 out of 5" title="4 out of 5" width="135" height="15" style="margin-left:-15px" />
</div></div>
<div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" class="BVRRRatingNormalOutOf"> <span itemprop="ratingValue" class="BVRRNumber BVRRRatingNumber">4</span>
<span class="BVRRSeparatorText">out of</span>
<span itemprop="bestRating" class="BVRRNumber BVRRRatingRangeNumber">5</span>
</div></div></div></div> </div>
<div class="RRReviewDisplayStyle2BeforeContentContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRReviewDisplayStyle2ContentContainer">
<div class="BVRRReviewTextContainer"><div class="BVRRReviewTextParagraph BVRRReviewTextFirstParagraph BVRRReviewTextLastParagraph"><span itemprop="description" class="BVRRReviewText">We bought this seat to use as the primary seat for our daughter. The seat shipped and arrived very quickly. After reading other reviews I knew that it was a larger seat so I was ok with that - we have a Toyota Rav4 and it fits fine (currently it is in the middle, rear facing). I'm able to still sit on the side with plenty of room. My daughter seems to like the seat - it seems very cushy and comfy. The buckle is a little cumbersome as it snaps more in and up then straight in so it does take a moment longer to get her buckled into the seat. Also, it is very hard to tighten the belts once the seat is installed (this is why I didn't rate it 5 stars). Overall a great seat for the price also like the built in cup holders for when she gets a bit older (right now it is a great pacifier holder)!</span></div></div>
<div class="RRRBeforeSecondaryRatingsContainerSpacer"></div>

<div class="BVRRUserNicknameContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserNicknamePrefix">By </span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRUserNickname"><span itemprop="author" class="BVRRNickname">Lyrik </span></span> <span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserNicknameSuffix">,</span>
<div class="BVRRUserLocationContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserLocationPrefix"></span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRUserLocation">LOUISIANA</span><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserLocationSuffix"></span></div></div>
<div class="BVRROverallRatingContainer" >
<div class="BVRRRatingContainerStar"><div class="BVRRRatingEntry BVRROdd"><div id="BVRRRatingOverall_Review_Display" class="BVRRRating BVRRRatingNormal BVRRRatingOverall"><div class="BVRRLabel BVRRRatingNormalLabel"></div><div class="BVRRRatingNormalImage">
<div class="BVImgOrSprite" style="width:75px;height:15px;overflow:hidden"><img src="http://walmart.ugc.bazaarvoice.com/1336/5_0/9/rating.png" alt="5 out of 5" title="5 out of 5" width="135" height="15" />
</div></div>
<div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" class="BVRRRatingNormalOutOf"> <span itemprop="ratingValue" class="BVRRNumber BVRRRatingNumber">5</span>
<span class="BVRRSeparatorText">out of</span>
<span itemprop="bestRating" class="BVRRNumber BVRRRatingRangeNumber">5</span>
</div></div></div></div> </div>
<div class="RRReviewDisplayStyle2BeforeContentContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRReviewDisplayStyle2ContentContainer">
<div class="BVRRReviewTextContainer"><div class="BVRRReviewTextParagraph BVRRReviewTextFirstParagraph BVRRReviewTextLastParagraph"><span itemprop="description" class="BVRRReviewText">I searched for a new seat for my 8 month old baby (18 1/2 lbs), for @ least 2 months before finally settling on this one. I wanted something safe, comfortable, not too expensive &amp; rear facing. I luv this seat! Though the material is not as soft as it looks in the picture, I still like it. My baby looks soooo comfortable in this seat!. I was worried because all the reviews that I read labeled this seat large, which made me nervous because I have a 5 year old who still uses a highback booster &amp; I drive a 2010 chevy malibu. This was ok. I was able to fit both my babies in the back plus a medium sized adult &amp; was still able to have a front seat passenger! ( the graco my ride was in the middle). The seat is bulky, but it is okay, I ride with the seat strapped behind my passenger seat &amp; it is really secure. My baby takes a nap on almost every ride! I would recommend this seat to anyone, and if you are like me &amp; are nervous about the size, just try it out, &amp; if it doesn't work then return it. It is definately worth a try!</span></div></div>

<div class="BVRRReviewTitleContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewTitlePrefix"></span> <h2>
<span itemprop="name" class="BVRRValue BVRRReviewTitle">Great Car Seat, Great Price</span> </h2>
<span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewTitleSuffix">,</span></div>
<div class="BVRRReviewDateContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewDatePrefix"></span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRReviewDate">07/12/2012<meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2012-07-12"/></span><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewDateSuffix"></span></div>
<div class="RRBeforeUserContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRUserNicknameContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserNicknamePrefix">By </span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRUserNickname"><span itemprop="author" class="BVRRNickname">MommaBeMe </span></span> <span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserNicknameSuffix">,</span>
<div class="BVRRUserLocationContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserLocationPrefix"></span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRUserLocation">Traverse City, MI</span><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserLocationSuffix"></span></div></div>
<div class="BVRROverallRatingContainer" >
<div class="BVRRRatingContainerStar"><div class="BVRRRatingEntry BVRROdd"><div id="BVRRRatingOverall_Review_Display" class="BVRRRating BVRRRatingNormal BVRRRatingOverall"><div class="BVRRLabel BVRRRatingNormalLabel"></div><div class="BVRRRatingNormalImage">
<div class="BVImgOrSprite" style="width:75px;height:15px;overflow:hidden"><img src="http://walmart.ugc.bazaarvoice.com/1336/5_0/9/rating.png" alt="5 out of 5" title="5 out of 5" width="135" height="15" />
</div></div>
<div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" class="BVRRRatingNormalOutOf"> <span itemprop="ratingValue" class="BVRRNumber BVRRRatingNumber">5</span>
<span class="BVRRSeparatorText">out of</span>
<span itemprop="bestRating" class="BVRRNumber BVRRRatingRangeNumber">5</span>
</div></div></div></div> </div>
<div class="RRReviewDisplayStyle2BeforeContentContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRReviewDisplayStyle2ContentContainer">
<div class="BVRRReviewTextContainer"><div class="BVRRReviewTextParagraph BVRRReviewTextFirstParagraph BVRRReviewTextLastParagraph"><span itemprop="description" class="BVRRReviewText">I purchased this car seat after researching for a few months. My daughter had always hated her infant car seat and she seemed so uncomfortable in it. So I purchased this one because it looked very comfy and the safety ratings were excellent. Things I love about this seat, the pattern and colors, the large cup holders, straps are easily adjusted, the height and weight limit are the best you will find in a convertible seat, and the seat is pretty easy to install. My 6 month old daughter loves this seat because its like an over sized recliner for her. Two things I dislike about the seat is that in my GMC Envoy it is hard to get it positioned in a level spot, the other thing is that the seat is large so anyone who is tall can't ride in the seat in front of where my daughter sits. Over all I love the seat and I am very happy with it.</span></div></div>
<div class="RRRBeforeSecondaryRatingsContainerSpacer"></div>

<div class="BVRRReviewTitleContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewTitlePrefix"></span> <h2>
<span itemprop="name" class="BVRRValue BVRRReviewTitle">Love this seat!</span> </h2>
<span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewTitleSuffix">,</span></div>
<div class="BVRRReviewDateContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewDatePrefix"></span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRReviewDate">07/10/2012<meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2012-07-10"/></span><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRReviewDateSuffix"></span></div>
<div class="RRBeforeUserContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRUserNicknameContainer"><span class="BVRRLabel BVRRUserNicknamePrefix">By </span><span class="BVRRValue BVRRUserNickname"><span itemprop="author" class="BVRRNickname">tifdesign </span></span></div>
<div class="BVRROverallRatingContainer" >
<div class="BVRRRatingContainerStar"><div class="BVRRRatingEntry BVRROdd"><div id="BVRRRatingOverall_Review_Display" class="BVRRRating BVRRRatingNormal BVRRRatingOverall"><div class="BVRRLabel BVRRRatingNormalLabel"></div><div class="BVRRRatingNormalImage">
<div class="BVImgOrSprite" style="width:75px;height:15px;overflow:hidden"><img src="http://walmart.ugc.bazaarvoice.com/1336/5_0/9/rating.png" alt="5 out of 5" title="5 out of 5" width="135" height="15" />
</div></div>
<div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" class="BVRRRatingNormalOutOf"> <span itemprop="ratingValue" class="BVRRNumber BVRRRatingNumber">5</span>
<span class="BVRRSeparatorText">out of</span>
<span itemprop="bestRating" class="BVRRNumber BVRRRatingRangeNumber">5</span>
</div></div></div></div> </div>
<div class="RRReviewDisplayStyle2BeforeContentContainerSpacer"></div>
<div class="BVRRReviewDisplayStyle2ContentContainer">
<div class="BVRRReviewTextContainer"><div class="BVRRReviewTextParagraph BVRRReviewTextFirstParagraph BVRRReviewTextLastParagraph"><span itemprop="description" class="BVRRReviewText">Bought this for my 6 mo. daughter who was outgrowing her carrier. I love this seat! It is rather large, but it's very well built and roomy. My lo loves this seat and its nice when she falls asleep in the car and I don't have to worry about &quot;floppy head&quot; because it has quite a bit of a recline to it. It is a little hard to get in and out of but I think that is to be expected with most car seats. I love that she will be able to rear face til 40 lbs. Great buy for the money.</span></div></div>
<div class="RRRBeforeSecondaryRatingsContainerSpacer"></div>
